   vyākhyāsyannādāvatiśayokterudāharaṇamāha  yathā tānītyādi /	vyAKyAsyan= AdO= atiSaya ukteH udAharaNam Aha  yaTA tAni ityAdi /
   "nidrārdhamīlitaddaśo madamantharāṇi nāpyarthavanti na ca yāni	"nidrA arDa mIlita ddaSaH mada manTarANi na api arTavanti na ca yAni
   nirarthakāni adyāpi me mṛgaddaśo madhurāṇi tasyāḥ" ityādyapādatrayam /	nirarTakAni adya api me mRgaddaSaH maDurANi tasyAH" iti Adya pAda trayam /
   atiśayoktyānayetyasya vyākhyānaṃ   atiśayoktyānākhyeyatoktyeti /	atiSaya ukti Anaya iti asya vyAKyAnaM   atiSaya uktyA anAKyeya toktyA iti /

   darśitam /	darSitam /

   sarvasyāpi paramaśivasvarūpatvābhisamdhānenopasaṃharati   iti śivamiti /	sarvasya api parama Siva svarUpa tva aBisamDAnena upasaMharati   iti Sivam iti /
   itītyanena svavyākhyānaparāmarśaḥ /	iti iti anena sva vyAKyAna parAmarSaH /
   kiñca śivamitīśvaranirdeśarūpaṃ paramaṃ maṅgalam /	kiQca Sivam iti ISvara nirdeSa rUpam paramam maFgalam /
   svarūpamākhyāyate tatte 'pi yuktābhidhāyina eva //	svarUpam AKyAyate tat te api yukta aBiDAyinaH eva //
   locana.m kiṃ locanaṃ vināloko bhāti candrikayāpi hi /	locana.m kim locanam vinA AlokaH BAti candrikayA api hi /
   tenābhinavagupto 'tra locanonmīlanaṃ vyadhāt //	tena aBinavaguptaH atra locana unmIlanam vyaDAt //

   iti śrīmahāmāheśvarācāryavaryābhinavaguptonmīlite sahṛdayālokalocane	iti SrI mahA mAheSvara AcArya varya aBinavagupta unmIlite sahRdaya Aloka locane
   dhvanisaṅkete prathama uddyotaḥ //	Dvani saFkete praTamaH uddyotaH //
             bālapriyā svavyākhyāne śrotṛjanapravṛtyarthamāha  kimityādi /	     bAla priyA sva vyAKyAne SrotR jana pravRti arTam Aha  kim ityAdi /
   locanaṃ locanākhyametadvyākhyānam /	locanam locana AKyam etat vyAKyAnam /

   candrikayā anyakṛtayā candrikākhyavyākhyayā /	candrikayA anya kRtayA candrikA AKya vyAKyayA /
   api kiṃ bhāti na bhātītyarthaḥ /	api kim BAti na BAti iti arTaH /

   atha ca locanaṃ netraṃ vinā /	aTa ca locanam netram vinA /
   lokaḥ bhūvanam /	lokaH BUvanam /
   candrikayā jyotsnayā, api kiṃ bhāti kiṃ sphurati na pratyakṣaviṣayo	candrikayA jyotsnayA, api kim BAti kim sPurati na pratyakza vizayaH

   yasyāḥ śakteḥ unmīlanayuktyā spandanayogainaiva /	yasyAH SakteH unmIlana yuktyA spandana yoga ena eva /
   viśvaṃ sarvaṃ vastu /	viSvam sarvam vastu /
   kṣaṇādunmīlati prakāśate /	kzaNAt unmIlati prakASate /
   kṣaṇādityanenānanyāpekṣatvaṃ dyotyate /	kzaNAt iti anena ananyA apekza tvam dyotyate /
   svātmani svasvarūpe /	sva Atmani sva svarUpe /
   yadvā  brahyacaitanya evāyatane sthāne viśrāntāṃ sthitām /	yat vA   brahya cEtanyaH eva Ayatane sTAne viSrAntAm sTitAm /
   pratibhāṃ jñānātmikām /	pratiBAm jQAna AtmikAm /
   śivāṃ śivākhyām /	SivAm Siva AKyAm /
   tāṃ śaktimahaṃ vande /	tAm Saktim aham vande /
   atha ca yasyāḥ pratibhāyāḥ unmīlanayuktyā prakāśayogena /	aTa ca yasyAH pratiBAyAH unmIlana yuktyA prakASa yogena /
   viśvam kṣaṇādunmīlati navanavatayā bhāti svātmanyevāyatane viśrāntāṃ	viSvam kzaNAt unmIlati nava nava tayA BAti sva Atmani eva Ayatane viSrAntAm
   vāsanārūpeṇāvasthitām, śivāṃ rasāveśavaiśadyasubhagām, tāṃ pratibhāṃ	vAsanA rUpeNa avasTitAm, SivAm rasa AveSa vESadya suBagAm, tAm pratiBAm

   prauḍhaṃ kva locanaṃ mandaḥ kvāhaṃ tena mayā kṛtā /	prOXam kva locanam mandaH kva aham tena mayA kRtA /
